< review>
Relic Vintage is quite literally the store of my dreams; I never knew something so perfect could actually exist until I walked in and saw it all for myself. To start I'd like to say the clothing selection is amazing. Every piece there is desirable and beautiful and made at a high standard that is quite frankly missing in clothing nowadays. I got chills from touching some of the gorgeous pieces. I could definitely spend hours in this store simply marveling at everything. For women there is a generous selection of pieces ranging from beautiful party dresses to irresistible pedal pusher capris. As I was browsing, my mouth agape, I was immediately approached by Oran and he started a dressing room for me. Oran gave me the best service, by far, that I've ever had at a store. I'd find a pair of pants and he'd know just the thing that would go with him. He brought me countless beautiful party dresses to try on and very single one of them fit me perfectly and were something that I loved and would pick out myself. And same for the friend I was with. He appears to have a talent for figuring out people's size and taste in dress without even asking. I wish everyone who worked in stores were like Oran. I will definitely be returning very soon. If you have a chance to go to Relic Vintage, do not pass it up! Everything about this store is unbelievably amazing.<//review>

Relic Vintage is unlike any other vintage store that I have ever been to and I am a diehard vintage-enthusiast. The selection is impeccable, curated by the fabulous owner, Oran, who has an eye for top quality vintage and prices his pieces affordably. I think the best part about shopping here is knowing that Oran will take the time to fit you into a perfect look and provide a unique shopping experience. I wish he could be my personal stylist! So many times, I have gone into vintage stores only to feel like I was rummaging at a yard sale and that is NOT the case here. Everything is in really good shape because Oran is a tailor, as well, and can fix any piece! Amazing! In fact, there was one dress I had my eye on but was far too tight, and he was able to transform it to fit me perfectly. I cannot recommend Relic Vintage enough! I tell all of my friends and family to shop here and bring my girls in for a fun time trying on clothes. In fact, Oran fitted out my bridesmaids for my wedding and they all looked AMAZING.<//review>

Inconsistent with portion size verses other locations. Ordered two orders of the 2 piece  chicken combos with  2  side orders with drinks. The pieces of chicken appeared the smallest I have ever bought before , they appeared to be from baby chicks with just a thin layer of chicken.  Had to talk to the manager who admitted this has happeneld all day. Other customers who overheard my complaints mentioned they should of complained as well, earlier. If that wasn't enough the soda dispenser was giving out only carbonated colored soda water and the counter sales person admitted she was aware of this but two other employers were responsible for that and hadn't got around to it yet. After demanding to speak with the manager I over heard two other employees laugh as to how many people had taken their orders out and with todays heat of 104 degrees how funny was that to them, {speaking in spanish} ,assuming  that I didn't understand and assuming I wasn't bi-lingual...When they finally got around to
getting that  corrected the ice dispenser didn't work and the other beverages stopped working.
